45536 - Modified G-67 Nexus Chip This small data chip stores the key elements of a ship's artificial intelligence system, and is used primarily for controlling the vessel's autonomous functions. This particular chip has been heavily modified by outlaw scientists, using technology that appears to have been salvaged from derelict Jovian outposts.

Advanced starship technology of this kind may be valuable to the right buyers. Rumors spreading through New Eden's underworld suggest that brokers operating out of the dangerous N-K4Q0 constellation have been inquiring about nexus chips matching this description.		 Miscellaneous

45544 - Standup M-Set Thukker Capital Component Manufacturing Material Efficiency This rig has been optimized for use in low security space and will provide reduced benefits in all other areas of space.

The Standup M-Set Thukker Capital Component Manufacturing Material Efficiency rig provides a means for structure operators to decrease material requirements when manufacturing capital ship construction components in their Upwell structures.

This facility design has been modified by Thukker specialists to utilize certain unregulated opportunities for expediting capital ship component construction in low security space.

Standup is a proprietary system that uses a Structure Autonomous Nanoassembly Device (Upwell) containing integrated template software, a nanoassembler array and sufficient nanomass to enable the construction of a variety of service modules, structure modules and structure rigs when inserted into the appropriate slots on a structure built with Upwell technology.

Note: Only one rig of the same type, counting both tech variations, may be fitted at the same time on a structure.		 Structure Engineering Rig M - Basic Capital Component ME

45548 - Standup XL-Set Thukker Structure and Component Manufacturing Efficiency This rig has been optimized for use in low security space and will provide reduced benefits in all other areas of space. When installed in low security space it provides enhanced benefits to the materials required for construction of capital ship components and normal benefits to the construction of other components, Upwell structures, structure modules, structure rigs, starbase structures and fuel blocks.

The Standup XL-Set Thukker Structure and Component Manufacturing Efficiency rig provides a means for structure operators to decrease both material and time requirements manufacturing components, Upwell structures, structure modules, structure rigs, starbase structures and fuel blocks in their Upwell structures.

This facility design has been modified by Thukker specialists to utilize certain unregulated opportunities for expediting capital ship component construction in low security space.

Standup is a proprietary system that uses a Structure Autonomous Nanoassembly Device (Upwell) containing integrated template software, a nanoassembler array and sufficient nanomass to enable the construction of a variety of service modules, structure modules and structure rigs when inserted into the appropriate slots on a structure built with Upwell technology.

Removed Items (1 Entries)

TypeID & Name Description Group Attributes
45552 - Guristas Victory SKIN (Permanent) Super Kerr-Induced Nanocoatings (SKINs) are a technology that enables capsuleers to change the look of their ships at will. Individual ship SKINs are activated by integrating the special encoding into the pilot's neural interfaces, and are subsequently available to use on any suitable ship flown by the capsuleer.

This rare SKIN was designed and manufactured by the Independent Gaming Commission exclusively as a prize for alliances that achieved victory over their opponents in Alliance Tournament XII in YC117. This SKIN uses prototype adapters to enable its application to a number of related ship hulls using the same instruction set.		 Super Kerr-Induced Nanocoatings

128480 Ah so it's you, {[character]player.name}. You've made quite a name for yourself within the inner circles of the Empire, I'm sure you will come in handy. I have a few tasks that need to be carried out a.s.a.p., in the name of Joint Harvesting. Acquiring mercenaries in these parts has been quite difficult to say the least, considering the locals absolutely despise us. Their ungratefulness is astounding, considering how well we treated them during our reign over the Minmatar territories.

Well enough of that, I'll get to the point. We had a convoy incoming from the Amarrian territories to one of our plantations in Barkrik when disaster struck. A group of vile 'freedom fighter' terrorists ambushed them as soon as they appeared out of hyper-jump within Barkrik. The escort ships managed to fend off the attackers, allowing the freighter to escape relatively unharmed. But due to the interference, it went a little off course and ended up crashing into an area of deadspace we call 'The Dustbowl'. It's not far from here, and all travelers are advised to avoid it at all costs. What a stroke of bad luck for our convoy to end up in there!

Needless to say, we haven't heard from it since. The Dustbowl is infested with rogue drones and criminals hiding from the law. No sane person without a bounty on his head ventures in there, it's a virtual death trap. I'm certain our freighter has either been destroyed or so badly damaged that it can't escape. I want you to fly in there and investigate, if you find the freighter bring back anything you can salvage from it to me. And don't speak a word of your findings to anyone! Engineers, mechanics, scientists, these and other professions – when used directly to aid combatant forces – can be said to have justifiably draw the wrath of their enemies. There just enough shades of grey to allow it.

No empire, however, is foolish enough to outright murder citizens without any involvement in a conflict. Or as some might argue, they are not so foolish as to get caught in the act. 264064 Jump Bridges allow corporations to link two Starbases in nearby systems and establish an artificial jump corridor, granting instantaneous transit capability between the two.

Jump Bridges have a defined maximum range and cannot link to other Bridges outside this range. Failure condition: Your HP (2) reaches 0

You need to defeat defense nodes that are randomly scattered, which include 4 types:
- Firewall (3) , a standard defense system with high HP
- Anti-Virus (4), a standard defense system with high damage
- Restoration Node (5), when activated, restores HP of discovered defense systems
- Virus Suppressor (6), when activated, weakens damage you can cause

Utility subsystems can be found randomly, you can use them to break defense nodes or repair yourself.
- Self Repair (7), restores 5 HP each time for 3 in the following 3 steps
- Polymorphic Shield (8), protects you from 2 attacks
- Kernel Rot (9), halves the HP of a defense system or System Core

315662 The Postouvin system became known throughout New Eden during the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119, as the site of one of the four Kyonoke outbreaks and the venue for the Kyonoke Inquest itself.

On YC119.02.13, the Astral Mining corporation confirmed that it had lost contact with its RP4 prospecting facility located within an asteroid field in orbit of Postouvin IV.

On YC119.02.18, the Federal Intelligence Office declared an indefinite quarantine of the RP4 facility due to the presence of the Kyonoke biomolecule. This emergency action trapped some eight million miners, support workers and families within the installation.

By YC119.02.22, the presence of the Kyonoke Plague, transmitted by the Kyonoke biomolecule, was confirmed at four outbreak sites including Astral Mining's RP4 facility in Postouvin, the Muttokon II space elevator, the city of Myrskaa on Oijanen II, and the Genolution Biotech Facility orbiting Efu V Moon 1.

CONCORD charged the Society of Conscious Thought to organize the response and their H4-RP4 Kyonoke Inquest Keepstar in Postouvin became the center of New Eden at the height of the crisis.

The fate of the RP4 and H4-RP4 facilities and the other outbreak sites weighed heavily in the proceedings on the H4-RP4 facility. Ultimately, in the face of a localized outbreak in the delegation center itself, the Kyonoke Inquest was successful in synthesizing and testing an experimental counter-agent functioning as a vaccine and cure.

Although the H4-RP4 Kyonoke Inquest's development of a counter-agent to the Kyonoke biomolecule brought much-needed hope, events on the RP4 prospecting facility were dark indeed and over seven million succumbed to a particularly virulent outbreak, which some alleged was complicated by conditions within RP4 and a muddled response by Federal authorities.

In contrast, out of the more than 265 million present aboard the H4-RP4 Keepstar, a mere 307 died before emergency dissemination of the counter-agent saved the Kyonoke Inquest from disaster.		 The Postouvin system became known throughout New Eden during the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119, as the site of one of the four Kyonoke outbreaks and the venue for the Kyonoke Inquest itself.

On YC119.02.13, the Astral Mining corporation confirmed that it had lost contact with its RP4 prospecting facility located within an asteroid field in orbit of Postouvin IV.

On YC119.02.18, the Federal Intelligence Office declared an indefinite quarantine of the RP4 facility due to the presence of the Kyonoke biomolecule. This emergency action trapped some eight million miners, support workers and families within the installation.

By YC119.02.22, the presence of the Kyonoke Plague, transmitted by the Kyonoke biomolecule, was confirmed at four outbreak sites including Astral Mining's RP4 facility in Postouvin, the Muttokon II space elevator, the city of Myrskaa on Oijanen II, and the Genolution Biotech Facility orbiting Efu V Moon 1.

CONCORD charged the Society of Conscious Thought to organize the response and their H4-RP4 Kyonoke Inquest Keepstar in Postouvin became the center of New Eden at the height of the crisis.

The fate of the RP4 and H4-RP4 facilities and the other outbreak sites weighed heavily in the proceedings on the H4-RP4 facility. Ultimately, in the face of a localized outbreak in the delegation center itself, the Kyonoke Inquest was successful in synthesizing and testing an experimental counter-agent functioning as a vaccine and cure.

Although the H4-RP4 Kyonoke Inquest's development of a counter-agent to the Kyonoke biomolecule brought much-needed hope, events on the RP4 prospecting facility were dark indeed and over seven million succumbed to a particularly virulent outbreak, which some alleged was complicated by conditions within RP4 and a muddled response by Federal authorities.

In contrast, out of the more than 265 million present aboard the H4-RP4 Keepstar, a mere 307 died before emergency dissemination of the counter-agent saved the Kyonoke Inquest from disaster.
315663 The Oijanen system had the misfortune to be the location of the most serious and tragic of the four outbreaks that made up the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119.

On YC119.02.09, reports emerged of the quarantine of a Zainou Biotech-owned medical facility located on Oijanen II, in the City of Myrskaa's District 36. Reports indicated that a survivor from a crashed frigate had earlier been taken to the District 36 South Medical Center.

On YC119.02.11, a combined force of State Peacekeepers, Home Guard and Caldari Navy elements sealed off the City of Myrskaa on Oijanen II, trapping some 36 million citizens under quarantine nanoshield domes.

By YC119.02.22, the presence of the Kyonoke Plague, transmitted by the Kyonoke biomolecule, was confirmed at four outbreak sites including the city of Myrskaa on Oijanen II, the Muttokon II space elevator, the Genolution Biotech Facility in orbiting Efu V Moon 1, and Astral Mining's RP4 facility in Postouvin.

CONCORD charged the Society of Conscious Thought to organize the response and their H4-RP4 Kyonoke Inquest Keepstar in Postouvin became the center of New Eden at the height of the crisis.

The fate of the City of Myrskaa and the other outbreak sites weighed heavily in the proceedings on the H4-RP4 facility. Ultimately, the Kyonoke Inquest was successful in synthesizing and testing an experimental counter-agent functioning as a vaccine and cure.

The development of a counter-agent to the Kyonoke biomolecule at the H4-RP4 Inquest Center came far too late for millions of Myrskaan citizens. A city of over 36 million was swept by a storm of plague and the ruthless but necessary containment. While the emergency deployment of the Kyonoke Inquest's counter-agent saved over 21 million inhabitants, it is understood that at least 14 million succumbed to the plague.

The Caldari State-sponsored Vital Secrets Act obscured the precise fate of approximately 1 million citizens unaccounted for after the crisis passed. All the lost of Myrskaa will be remembered alongside all those who died during the Kyonoke Crisis YC119.		 The Oijanen system had the misfortune to be the location of the most serious and tragic of the four outbreaks that made up the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119.

On YC119.02.09, reports emerged of the quarantine of a Zainou Biotech-owned medical facility located on Oijanen II, in the City of Myrskaa's District 36. Reports indicated that a survivor from a crashed frigate had earlier been taken to the District 36 South Medical Center.

315664 The Muttokon system was the locale of the first signs of a grave emergency that was to become the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119.

On YC119.02.08, the Muttokon II Freedom Extension Space Elevator was placed under quarantine within a tight security cordon ordered by the Republic Security Services.

On YC119.02.10, the Muttokon II incident was marked as a Class A Full Closure Quarantine and the elevator's orbital platform and tether were separated from the planetary anchor by order of Valkear General Heder Elislar.

By YC119.02.22, the presence of the Kyonoke Plague, transmitted by the Kyonoke biomolecule, was confirmed at four outbreak sites including the Muttokon II space elevator, the city of Myrskaa on Oijanen II, the Genolution Biotech Facility orbiting Efu V Moon 1, and Astral Mining's RP4 facility in Postouvin.

CONCORD charged the Society of Conscious Thought to organize the response and their H4-RP4 Kyonoke Inquest Keepstar in Postouvin became the center of New Eden at the height of the crisis.

The fate of the Muttokon II orbital platform and the other outbreak sites weighed heavily in the proceedings on the H4-RP4 facility. Ultimately, the Kyonoke Inquest was successful in synthesizing and testing an experimental counter-agent functioning as a vaccine and cure.

The orbital platform was flushed with the counter-agent and the process of recovery and rescue of over 700,000 survivors was a success for Freedom Extension and the Minmatar Republic. Even so, some 230,000 others aboard the platform died before the cure was discovered and are remembered among the dead of the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119. 315665 The Efu system became notable as the site of an outbreak of the Kyonoke Plague during the Kyonoke Crisis and Inquest YC119.

On YC119.02.12, the Genolution corporation confirmed that it had sealed off nine decks of its Biotech Production Facility in orbit of Efu V Moon 1, citing an unidentified pathogen.

On YC119.02.20, the Society of Conscious Thought confirmed that the presence of the Kyonoke biomolecule had been detected in the quarantined decks zone of the Genolution Biotech Facility and that some 65,000 had succumbed to a form of the Kyonoke Plague.

The fate of the Genolution Biotech Facility and the other outbreak sites weighed heavily in the proceedings on the H4-RP4 facility. Ultimately, the Kyonoke Inquest was successful in synthesizing and testing an experimental counter-agent functioning as a vaccine and cure.

After the development of a counter-agent, the Society of Conscious Thought implemented the Amarr Empire-sponsored Cure Act and treated everyone aboard the station, both within the quarantine zone and outside it. Although over 370,000 people within the cordon had died, to be remembered with the other dead of the Kyonoke Crisis, the remaining 359,000 were successfully treated. 522634 Super Kerr-Induced Nanocoatings (SKINs) are a technology that enables capsuleers to change the look of their ships at will. Individual ship SKINs are activated by integrating the special encoding into the pilot's neural interfaces, and are subsequently available to use on any suitable ship flown by the capsuleer.

This rare SKIN was designed and manufactured by the Independent Gaming Commission exclusively as a prize for alliances that achieved victory over their opponents in Alliance Tournament XIV in YC119. This SKIN uses prototype adapters to enable its application to a number of related ship hulls using the same instruction set. 526394 Standup M-Set Thukker Capital Component Manufacturing Material Efficiency Standup M-Set Thukker Capital Component Manufacturing Material Efficiency Item name for typeID 45544 (Structure Engineering Rig M - Basic Capital Component ME)
526395 This rig has been optimized for use in low security space and will provide reduced benefits in all other areas of space.

The Standup M-Set Thukker Capital Component Manufacturing Material Efficiency rig provides a means for structure operators to decrease material requirements when manufacturing capital ship construction components in their Upwell structures.

This facility design has been modified by Thukker specialists to utilize certain unregulated opportunities for expediting capital ship component construction in low security space.

Standup is a proprietary system that uses a Structure Autonomous Nanoassembly Device (Upwell) containing integrated template software, a nanoassembler array and sufficient nanomass to enable the construction of a variety of service modules, structure modules and structure rigs when inserted into the appropriate slots on a structure built with Upwell technology.

Note: Only one rig of the same type, counting both tech variations, may be fitted at the same time on a structure.		 This rig has been optimized for use in low security space and will provide reduced benefits in all other areas of space.
